Source was called directly","+  # placeholder for direct execution"," }"]}],"originalFile":"###############################################################################\n# Adaptive Rejection Sampling (ARS)\n# Based on: Gilks, W. R., & Wild, P. (1992). Adaptive rejection sampling\n#           for Gibbs sampling. JRSS Series C, 41(2), 337-348.\n#\n# File: /app/ars.R\n###############################################################################\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: evaluate log-density safely (vectorized)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\neval_log_density <- function(f, x) {\n  # f is the unnormalized density; we return log(f(x))\n  fx <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.nan(fx) | is.na(fx))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NaN/NA values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(fx < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  log_fx <- ifelse(fx > 0, log(fx), -Inf)\n  return(log_fx)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: compute derivative of h = log(f) via finite differences\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ncompute_derivative <- function(h_vals, x_vals) {\n  n <- length(x_vals)\n  if (n < 2) stop(\"Need at least 2 abscissae to compute derivatives.\")\n  dh <- diff(h_vals) / diff(x_vals)\n  return(dh)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: check log-concavity of h at the current abscissae\n# Returns TRUE if log-concave, FALSE otherwise\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(h_vals, x_vals) {\n  n <- length(x_vals)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)  # can't check with fewer than 3 points\n  dh <- compute_derivative(h_vals, x_vals)\n  # Log-concavity requires that the slopes are non-increasing\n  for (i in 2:length(dh)) {\n    if (dh[i] > dh[i - 1] + 1e-8) {\n      return(FALSE)\n    }\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: build the upper hull (piecewise linear envelope)\n# Returns a list with slopes, intercepts, and intersection points z\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nbuild_upper_hull <- function(h_vals, x_vals, lb, ub) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n\n  # Tangent lines: u_j(x) = h(x_j) + h'(x_j) * (x - x_j)\n  # We approximate h'(x_j) using secant slopes from neighbors\n  slopes <- numeric(k)\n  intercepts <- numeric(k)\n\n  if (k == 1) {\n    # Degenerate case: can't build a proper envelope with one point\n    stop(\"Need at least 2 abscissae to build the envelope.\")\n  }\n\n  # Slopes of secant lines between consecutive points\n  sec_slopes <- diff(h_vals) / diff(x_vals)\n\n  # For the upper hull in ARS (Gilks & Wild), we use the secant-based\n\n  # piecewise linear upper envelope:\n  # u_j(x) defined on [z_{j-1}, z_j] by the line through (x_j, h(x_j)) and (x_{j+1}, h(x_{j+1}))\n  # But actually the standard ARS uses tangent lines. Since we don't have the exact derivative,\n  # we use the formulation from the paper directly:\n  #\n  # The upper hull u(x) on interval [z_{j-1}, z_j] is defined by:\n  # u_j(x) = ((x_{j+1} - x)*h(x_j) + (x - x_j)*h(x_{j+1})) / (x_{j+1} - x_j)\n  # for j = 1, ..., k-1\n  #\n  # The intersection points z_j for j = 1, ..., k-2 are where u_j = u_{j+1}\n  # z_0 = lb, z_{k-1} = ub\n\n  # Intersection points z\n  # z_j = (h(x_{j+1}) - h(x_j) + x_j * sec_j - x_{j+1} * sec_{j+1}) / (sec_j - sec_{j+1})\n  # where sec_j = (h(x_{j+1}) - h(x_j)) / (x_{j+1} - x_j)\n\n  # Actually, let's use the tangent-line formulation properly.\n  # For each interior point, the derivative is approximated.\n  # For endpoints, we use one-sided differences.\n\n  # Derivative approximation at each abscissa\n  hprime <- numeric(k)\n  if (k == 2) {\n    # Both points get the same slope (secant)\n    hprime[1] <- sec_slopes[1]\n    hprime[2] <- sec_slopes[1]\n  } else {\n    # First point: if lb is -Inf, the slope must be positive for integrability\n    hprime[1] <- sec_slopes[1]\n    # Last point: if ub is Inf, the slope must be negative for integrability\n    hprime[k] <- sec_slopes[k - 1]\n    # Interior points: average of left and right secant slopes\n    for (j in 2:(k - 1)) {\n      hprime[j] <- (sec_slopes[j - 1] + sec_slopes[j]) / 2\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Check boundary conditions for integrability\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && lb < 0) {\n    if (hprime[1] <= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have positive slope at the leftmost abscissa when lb = -Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n  if (is.infinite(ub) && ub > 0) {\n    if (hprime[k] >= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have negative slope at the rightmost abscissa when ub = Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Tangent lines: u_j(x) = h(x_j) + hprime_j * (x - x_j)\n  # => u_j(x) = (h(x_j) - hprime_j * x_j) + hprime_j * x\n  # => intercept_j = h(x_j) - hprime_j * x_j, slope_j = hprime_j\n  for (j in 1:k) {\n    slopes[j] <- hprime[j]\n    intercepts[j] <- h_vals[j] - hprime[j] * x_vals[j]\n  }\n\n  # Intersection points z between consecutive tangent lines\n  # z_j: tangent j and tangent j+1 intersect\n  # slopes[j]*z + intercepts[j] = slopes[j+1]*z + intercepts[j+1]\n  # z = (intercepts[j+1] - intercepts[j]) / (slopes[j] - slopes[j+1])\n  z <- numeric(k + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[k + 1] <- ub\n  if (k >= 2) {\n    for (j in 1:(k - 1)) {\n      denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n      if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n        # Parallel tangent lines — place z at midpoint\n        z[j + 1] <- (x_vals[j] + x_vals[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- (intercepts[j + 1] - intercepts[j]) / denom\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return(list(\n    slopes = slopes,\n    intercepts = intercepts,\n    z = z,\n    hprime = hprime\n  ))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: build the lower hull (piecewise linear)\n# The lower hull l(x) = ((x_{j+1} - x)*h(x_j) + (x - x_j)*h(x_{j+1})) / (x_{j+1} - x_j)\n# for x in [x_j, x_{j+1}], and l(x) = -Inf outside [x_1, x_k]\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\neval_lower_hull <- function(x, h_vals, x_vals) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (x < x_vals[1] || x > x_vals[k]) {\n    return(-Inf)\n  }\n  # Find which interval x falls in\n  j <- findInterval(x, x_vals, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  if (j == 0) j <- 1\n  if (j >= k) j <- k - 1\n  # Linear interpolation\n  t <- (x - x_vals[j]) / (x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j])\n  return((1 - t) * h_vals[j] + t * h_vals[j + 1])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: sample from the piecewise exponential upper envelope\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nsample_upper_hull <- function(upper_hull) {\n  slopes <- upper_hull$slopes\n  intercepts <- upper_hull$intercepts\n  z <- upper_hull$z\n  k <- length(slopes)\n\n  # Compute the integral of exp(u(x)) on each piece [z_j, z_{j+1}]\n  # u_j(x) = slopes[j]*x + intercepts[j]\n  # integral = exp(intercepts[j]) * integral of exp(slopes[j]*x) dx from z[j] to z[j+1]\n\n  log_areas <- numeric(k)\n  for (j in 1:k) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    s <- slopes[j]\n    c <- intercepts[j]\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      # s must be > 0 for convergence\n      # integral from -Inf to b = exp(c) * exp(s*b) / s\n      log_areas[j] <- c + s * b - log(s)\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      # s must be < 0 for convergence\n      # integral from a to Inf = exp(c) * exp(s*a) / (-s)\n      log_areas[j] <- c + s * a - log(-s)\n    } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n      # Nearly flat: integral ~ exp(c) * (b - a)\n      log_areas[j] <- c + log(b - a)\n    } else {\n      # integral = exp(c) / s * (exp(s*b) - exp(s*a))\n      # = exp(c + s*a) / s * (exp(s*(b-a)) - 1)    [for numerical stability]\n      log_areas[j] <- c + s * a + log(abs(expm1(s * (b - a)))) - log(abs(s))\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Normalize to get probabilities for each piece\n  max_log <- max(log_areas)\n  areas <- exp(log_areas - max_log)\n  probs <- areas / sum(areas)\n\n  # Sample which piece\n  j <- sample.int(k, size = 1, prob = probs)\n\n  # Sample from the exponential distribution on piece j\n  a <- z[j]\n  b <- z[j + 1]\n  s <- slopes[j]\n  u <- runif(1)\n\n  if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n    # CDF: F(x) = exp(s*(x - b)) for x <= b, s > 0\n    # x = b + log(u) / s\n    x_star <- b + log(u) / s\n  } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n    # CDF: F(x) = 1 - exp(s*(x - a)) for x >= a, s < 0\n    # x = a + log(1 - u) / s   (note s < 0 so this gives x > a)\n    # Actually: x = a - log(1 - u) / (-s) = a + log(1-u)/s\n    x_star <- a + log(1 - u) / s\n  } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n    # Uniform on [a, b]\n    x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n  } else {\n    # General case: CDF from a to x\n    # F(x) = (exp(s*x) - exp(s*a)) / (exp(s*b) - exp(s*a))\n    # x = log(exp(s*a) + u*(exp(s*b) - exp(s*a))) / s\n    # For stability: let delta = s*(b-a)\n    # x = a + log(1 + u*(exp(delta) - 1)) / s\n    delta <- s * (b - a)\n    x_star <- a + log(1 + u * expm1(delta)) / s\n  }\n\n  # Evaluate upper hull at x_star\n  u_x <- s * x_star + intercepts[j]\n\n  return(list(x = x_star, u_x = u_x))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: validate inputs for the ars function\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub, x_init) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || n < 1 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be less than 'ub'.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.null(x_init)) {\n    if (!is.numeric(x_init) || length(x_init) < 2) {\n      stop(\"'x_init' must be a numeric vector with at least 2 elements.\")\n    }\n    if (any(x_init <= lb) || any(x_init >= ub)) {\n      stop(\"All initial abscissae must be strictly inside (lb, ub).\")\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: choose initial abscissae automatically\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nchoose_initial_abscissae <- function(f, lb, ub, n_init = 5) {\n  # Determine finite search bounds\n  left <- if (is.infinite(lb)) -10 else lb + 0.01 * (ub - lb)\n  right <- if (is.infinite(ub)) 10 else ub - 0.01 * (ub - lb)\n\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) {\n    left <- -10\n    right <- 10\n  }\n\n  # Try a grid and find where density is positive\n  grid <- seq(left, right, length.out = max(n_init * 10, 50))\n  fvals <- f(grid)\n  pos_idx <- which(fvals > 0)\n\n  if (length(pos_idx) < 2) {\n    stop(\"Could not find at least 2 points where f(x) > 0 in the search range.\")\n  }\n\n  # Select n_init evenly spaced points from the positive region\n  sel <- pos_idx[seq(1, length(pos_idx), length.out = min(n_init, length(pos_idx)))]\n  x_init <- grid[sel]\n\n  # Ensure we span the mode region - add the mode if we can find it\n  mode_idx <- which.max(fvals)\n  mode_x <- grid[mode_idx]\n  if (!(mode_x %in% x_init) && fvals[mode_idx] > 0) {\n    x_init <- sort(unique(c(x_init, mode_x)))\n  }\n\n  return(x_init)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Main function: Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, x_init = NULL) {\n  # --- Input Validation --- #\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub, x_init)\n\n  # --- Choose initial abscissae if not provided --- #\n  if (is.null(x_init)) {\n    x_init <- choose_initial_abscissae(f, lb, ub)\n  }\n  x_init <- sort(unique(x_init))\n\n  # --- Initialize abscissae and log-density values --- #\n  x_abs <- x_init\n  h_vals <- eval_log_density(f, x_abs)\n\n  # --- Check initial log-concavity --- #\n  if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n    stop(\"Density does not appear to be log-concave based on initial abscissae.\")\n  }\n\n  # --- Build initial upper hull --- #\n  upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n\n  # --- Sampling loop --- #\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  count <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100  # safety limit\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (count < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Step 1: Sample x* from the upper hull envelope\n    proposal <- sample_upper_hull(upper_hull)\n    x_star <- proposal$x\n    u_x_star <- proposal$u_x\n\n    # Step 2: Generate uniform for squeeze/rejection test\n    w <- runif(1)\n\n    # Step 3: Evaluate lower hull (squeeze test)\n    l_x_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, h_vals, x_abs)\n\n    if (log(w) <= l_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      # Accepted by squeeze test — no need to evaluate f\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n    } else {\n      # Step 4: Evaluate h(x*) = log(f(x*)) for rejection test\n      h_x_star <- eval_log_density(f, x_star)\n\n      if (log(w) <= h_x_star - u_x_star) {\n        # Accepted by rejection test\n        count <- count + 1\n        samples[count] <- x_star\n      }\n\n      # Step 5: Update the abscissae (add x* to the set)\n      ins_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n      h_vals <- append(h_vals, h_x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n\n      # Step 6: Check log-concavity with the new point\n      if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n        stop(\"Log-concavity violated after adding a new point. The density is not log-concave.\")\n      }\n\n      # Step 7: Rebuild the upper hull\n      upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (count < n) {\n    warning(paste(\"Only generated\", count, \"out of\", n, \"requested samples.\"))\n    samples <- samples[1:count]\n  }\n\n  return(samples)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Test function: formal testing with known distributions\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler — Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  # Helper: report result\n  report <- function(name, passed, info = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": PASS\"), \"\\n\")\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": FAIL\"), \"\\n\")\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(info) > 0) cat(\"  \", info, \"\\n\")\n  }\n\n  # ================================================================ #\n  # TEST 1: Standard Normal Distribution\n  # ================================================================ #\n  cat(\"--- Test 1: Standard Normal N(0,1) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf)\n    m <- mean(samples)\n    s <- sd(samples)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~0), SD = %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", m, s))\n    # KS test against true distribution\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pnorm\")\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m) < 0.1 && abs(s - 1) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n\n    # Save samples\n    writeLines(as.character(samples), \"/app/normal_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved 10000 samples to /app/normal_samples.txt\\n\")\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  # ================================================================ #\n  # TEST 2: Exponential Distribution (rate=1)\n  # ================================================================ #\n  cat(\"--- Test 2: Exponential(rate=1) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = dexp, lb = 0, ub = Inf,\n                   x_init = c(0.1, 1, 3, 5))\n    m <- mean(samples)\n    s <- sd(samples)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~1), SD = %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", m, s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pexp\")\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m - 1) < 0.15 && abs(s - 1) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_exponential_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n\n    # Save samples\n    writeLines(as.character(samples), \"/app/exponential_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved 10000 samples to /app/exponential_samples.txt\\n\")\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_exponential_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  # ================================================================ #\n  # TEST 3: Gamma Distribution (shape=3, rate=2)\n  # ================================================================ #\n  cat(\"--- Test 3: Gamma(shape=3, rate=2) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    f_gamma <- function(x) dgamma(x, shape = 3, rate = 2)\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = f_gamma, lb = 0, ub = Inf,\n                   x_init = c(0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 4))\n    m <- mean(samples)\n    s <- sd(samples)\n    true_mean <- 3 / 2  # shape/rate\n    true_sd <- sqrt(3) / 2  # sqrt(shape)/rate\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~%.4f), SD = %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\",\n                m, true_mean, s, true_sd))\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pgamma\", shape = 3, rate = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m - true_mean) < 0.15 && abs(s - true_sd) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_gamma_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_gamma_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  # hprime_j * (x - x_j) = intercept_j + slope_j * x\n  slopes <- hprime\n  intercepts <- h_vals - hprime * x_vals\n\n  # Intersection points z between consecutive tangent lines\n  z <- numeric(k + 1)\n   z[j + 1] <- (intercepts[j + 1] - intercepts[j]) / denom\n    }\n  }\n\n  return(list(slopes = slopes, intercepts = intercepts, z = z))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: evaluate the lower hull (chord through consecutive abscissae)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\neval_lower_hull <- function(x, h_vals, x_vals) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (x < x_vals[1] || x > x_vals[k]) return(-Inf)\n  j <- findInterval(x, x_vals, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  if (j == 0) j <- 1\n  if (j >= k) j <- k - 1\n  dx <- x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j]\n  if (abs(dx) < 1e-15) return(h_vals[j])\n  t <- (x - x_vals[j]) / dx\n  return((1 - t) * h_vals[j] + t * h_vals[j + 1])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: sample from the piecewise-exponential upper envelope\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nsample_upper_hull <- function(upper_hull) {\n  slopes <- upper_hull$slopes\n  intercepts <- upper_hull$intercepts\n  z <- upper_hull$z\n  k <- length(slopes)\n\n  # Compute log of the integral of exp(s*x + c) on each piece [a, b]\n  log_areas <- numeric(k)\n  for (j in 1:k) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    s <- slopes[j]\n    c_val <- intercepts[j]\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * b - log(s)\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a - log(-s)\n    } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + log(b - a)\n    } else {\n      # log(integral) = c + s*a + log(|expm1(s*(b-a))|) - log(|s|)\n      delta <- s * (b - a)\n      if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n        # Taylor approximation for small delta\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * (a + b) / 2 + log(b - a)\n      } else {\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a + log(abs(expm1(delta))) - log(abs(s))\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Filter out non-finite log_areas (shouldn't happen, but safety)\n  valid <- is.finite(log_areas)\n  if (!any(valid)) stop(\"All envelope pieces have non-finite area.\")\n\n  # Normalize to get probabilities\n  max_log <- max(log_areas[valid])\n  areas <- rep(0, k)\n  areas[valid] <- exp(log_areas[valid] - max_log)\n  probs <- areas / sum(areas)\n\n  # Sample which piece\n  j <- sample.int(k, size = 1, prob = probs)\n\n  a <- z[j]\n  b <- z[j + 1]\n  s <- slopes[j]\n  u <- runif(1)\n\n  if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n    x_star <- b + log(u) / s\n  } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n    x_star <- a + log(1 - u) / s\n  } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n    x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n  } else {\n    delta <- s * (b - a)\n    if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n      x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      x_star <- a + log(1 + u * expm1(delta)) / s\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Evaluate upper hull at x_star\n  u_x <- s * x_star + intercepts[j]\n  return(list(x = x_star, u_x = u_x))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: validate inputs\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub, x_init) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || n < 1 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be less than 'ub'.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.null(x_init)) {\n    if (!is.numeric(x_init) || length(x_init) < 2) {\n      stop(\"'x_init' must be a numeric vector with at least 2 elements.\")\n    }\n    if (any(x_init <= lb) || any(x_init >= ub)) {\n      stop(\"All initial abscissae must be strictly inside (lb, ub).\")\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: choose initial abscissae automatically\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nchoose_initial_abscissae <- function(f, lb, ub, n_init = 5) {\n  left <- if (is.infinite(lb)) -10 else lb + 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  right <- if (is.infinite(ub)) 10 else ub - 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) { left <- -10; right <- 10 }\n\n  grid <- seq(left, right, length.out = max(n_init * 10, 50))\n  fvals <- f(grid)\n  pos_idx <- which(fvals > 0)\n\n  if (length(pos_idx) < 2) {\n    stop(\"Could not find at least 2 points where f(x) > 0 in the search range.\")\n  }\n\n  sel <- pos_idx[seq(1, length(pos_idx), length.out = min(n_init, length(pos_idx)))]\n  x_init <- grid[sel]\n\n  mode_idx <- which.max(fvals)\n  mode_x <- grid[mode_idx]\n  if (!(mode_x %in% x_init) && fvals[mode_idx] > 0) {\n    x_init <- sort(unique(c(x_init, mode_x)))\n  }\n\n  return(x_init)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Main function: Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, x_init = NULL) {\n  # --- Input Validation --- #\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub, x_init)\n\n  # --- Choose initial abscissae if not provided --- #\n  if (is.null(x_init)) {\n    x_init <- choose_initial_abscissae(f, lb, ub)\n  }\n  x_init <- sort(unique(x_init))\n\n  # --- Initialize --- #\n  x_abs <- x_init\n  h_vals <- eval_log_density(f, x_abs)\n\n  # --- Check initial log-concavity --- #\n  if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n    stop(\"Density does not appear to be log-concave based on initial abscissae.\")\n  }\n\n  # --- Build initial upper hull --- #\n  upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n\n  # --- Sampling loop --- #\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  count <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (count < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Step 1: Sample from upper envelope\n    proposal <- sample_upper_hull(upper_hull)\n    x_star <- proposal$x\n    u_x_star <- proposal$u_x\n\n    # Safety: skip NaN proposals\n    if (!is.finite(x_star) || !is.finite(u_x_star)) next\n\n    # Step 2: Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    l_x_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, h_vals, x_abs)\n\n    if (is.finite(l_x_star) && log(w) <= l_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n      next\n    }\n\n    # Step 3: Rejection test — evaluate h(x*)\n    h_x_star <- eval_log_density(f, x_star)\n\n    if (log(w) <= h_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n    }\n\n    # Step 4: Update abscissae\n    ins_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n    x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n    h_vals <- append(h_vals, h_x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n\n    # Remove near-duplicates for numerical stability\n    dedup <- deduplicate_abscissae(x_abs, h_vals)\n    x_abs <- dedup$x\n    h_vals <- dedup$h\n\n    # Step 5: Check log-concavity\n    if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n      stop(\"Log-concavity violated after adding a new point. The density is not log-concave.\")\n    }\n\n    # Step 6: Rebuild upper hull\n    upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n  }\n\n  if (count < n) {\n    warning(paste(\"Only generated\", count, \"out of\", n, \"requested samples.\"))\n    samples <- samples[1:count]\n  }\n\n  return(samples)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Test function: formal testing with known distributions\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  report <- function(name, passed, info = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": PASS\"), \"\\n\")\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": FAIL\"), \"\\n\")\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(info) > 0) cat(\"  \", info, \"\\n\")\n  }\n\n  # R., & Wild, P. (1992). Adaptive rejection sampling\n#           for Gibbs sampling. JRSS Series C, 41(2), 337-348.\n#\n# File: /app/ars.R\n###############################################################################\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: evaluate log-density safely (vectorized)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\neval_log_density <- function(f, x) {\n  fx <- f(x)\n  if (any(is.nan(fx) | is.na(fx))) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned NaN/NA values.\")\n  }\n  if (any(fx < 0)) {\n    stop(\"Density function returned negative values. Density must be non-negative.\")\n  }\n  log_fx <- ifelse(fx > 0, log(fx), -Inf)\n  return(log_fx)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: check log-concavity at the current abscissae\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(h_vals, x_vals) {\n  n <- length(x_vals)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  dh <- diff(h_vals) / diff(x_vals)\n  # Log-concavity requires non-increasing slopes\n  for (i in 2:length(dh)) {\n    if (is.finite(dh[i]) && is.finite(dh[i - 1])) {\n      if (dh[i] > dh[i - 1] + 1e-6) {\n        return(FALSE)\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: remove near-duplicate abscissae to avoid numerical issues\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ndeduplicate_abscissae <- function(x_vals, h_vals, tol = 1e-10) {\n  keep <- rep(TRUE, length(x_vals))\n  for (i in 2:length(x_vals)) {\n    if (abs(x_vals[i] - x_vals[i - 1]) < tol) {\n      keep[i] <- FALSE\n    }\n  }\n  list(x = x_vals[keep], h = h_vals[keep])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: build the upper hull using secant-based tangent approximation\n#\n# Uses the formulation from Gilks & Wild (1992):\n# - For interior points j (2..k-1), the \"tangent\" slope at x_j is approximated\n#   by the slope of the line from (x_{j-1}, h_{j-1}) to (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1}).\n# - For endpoint j=1: slope of secant to x_2.\n# - For endpoint j=k: slope of secant from x_{k-1}.\n#\n# The intersection points z_j between consecutive tangent lines define the\n# piecewise domains.\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nbuild_upper_hull <- function(h_vals, x_vals, lb, ub) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (k < 2) stop(\"Need at least 2 abscissae to build the envelope.\")\n\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  sec <- diff(h_vals) / diff(x_vals)\n\n  # Approximate derivative at each abscissa\n  hprime <- numeric(k)\n  if (k == 2) {\n    hprime[1] <- sec[1]\n    hprime[2] <- sec[1]\n  } else {\n    hprime[1] <- sec[1]\n    hprime[k] <- sec[k - 1]\n    for (j in 2:(k - 1)) {\n      # Use slope through (x_{j-1}, h_{j-1}) and (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1})\n      hprime[j] <- (h_vals[j + 1] - h_vals[j - 1]) / (x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j - 1])\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Check boundary conditions for integrability\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && lb < 0) {\n    if (!is.finite(hprime[1]) || hprime[1] <= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have positive slope at the leftmost abscissa when lb = -Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n  if (is.infinite(ub) && ub > 0) {\n    if (!is.finite(hprime[k]) || hprime[k] >= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have negative slope at the rightmost abscissa when ub = Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Tangent lines: u_j(x) = h_j + hprime_j * (x - x_j) = intercept_j + slope_j * x\n  slopes <- hprime\n  intercepts <- h_vals - hprime * x_vals\n\n  # Intersection points z between consecutive tangent lines\n  z <- numeric(k + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[k + 1] <- ub\n  for (j in seq_len(k - 1)) {\n    denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n    if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n      z[j + 1] <- (x_vals[j] + x_vals[j + 1]) / 2\n    } else {\n      z[j + 1] <- (intercepts[j + 1] - intercepts[j]) / denom\n    }\n  }\n\n  return(list(slopes = slopes, intercepts = intercepts, z = z))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: evaluate the lower hull (chord through consecutive abscissae)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\neval_lower_hull <- function(x, h_vals, x_vals) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (x < x_vals[1] || x > x_vals[k]) return(-Inf)\n  j <- findInterval(x, x_vals, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  if (j == 0) j <- 1\n  if (j >= k) j <- k - 1\n  dx <- x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j]\n  if (abs(dx) < 1e-15) return(h_vals[j])\n  t <- (x - x_vals[j]) / dx\n  return((1 - t) * h_vals[j] + t * h_vals[j + 1])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: sample from the piecewise-exponential upper envelope\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nsample_upper_hull <- function(upper_hull) {\n  slopes <- upper_hull$slopes\n  intercepts <- upper_hull$intercepts\n  z <- upper_hull$z\n  k <- length(slopes)\n\n  # Compute log of the integral of exp(s*x + c) on each piece [a, b]\n  log_areas <- numeric(k)\n  for (j in 1:k) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    s <- slopes[j]\n    c_val <- intercepts[j]\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * b - log(s)\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a - log(-s)\n    } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + log(b - a)\n    } else {\n      # log(integral) = c + s*a + log(|expm1(s*(b-a))|) - log(|s|)\n      delta <- s * (b - a)\n      if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n        # Taylor approximation for small delta\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * (a + b) / 2 + log(b - a)\n      } else {\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a + log(abs(expm1(delta))) - log(abs(s))\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Filter out non-finite log_areas (shouldn't happen, but safety)\n  valid <- is.finite(log_areas)\n  if (!any(valid)) stop(\"All envelope pieces have non-finite area.\")\n\n  # Normalize to get probabilities\n  max_log <- max(log_areas[valid])\n  areas <- rep(0, k)\n  areas[valid] <- exp(log_areas[valid] - max_log)\n  probs <- areas / sum(areas)\n\n  # Sample which piece\n  j <- sample.int(k, size = 1, prob = probs)\n\n  a <- z[j]\n  b <- z[j + 1]\n  s <- slopes[j]\n  u <- runif(1)\n\n  if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n    x_star <- b + log(u) / s\n  } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n    x_star <- a + log(1 - u) / s\n  } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n    x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n  } else {\n    delta <- s * (b - a)\n    if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n      x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      x_star <- a + log(1 + u * expm1(delta)) / s\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Evaluate upper hull at x_star\n  u_x <- s * x_star + intercepts[j]\n  return(list(x = x_star, u_x = u_x))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: validate inputs\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub, x_init) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || n < 1 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be less than 'ub'.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.null(x_init)) {\n    if (!is.numeric(x_init) || length(x_init) < 2) {\n      stop(\"'x_init' must be a numeric vector with at least 2 elements.\")\n    }\n    if (any(x_init <= lb) || any(x_init >= ub)) {\n      stop(\"All initial abscissae must be strictly inside (lb, ub).\")\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: choose initial abscissae automatically\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nchoose_initial_abscissae <- function(f, lb, ub, n_init = 5) {\n  left <- if (is.infinite(lb)) -10 else lb + 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  right <- if (is.infinite(ub)) 10 else ub - 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) { left <- -10; right <- 10 }\n\n  grid <- seq(left, right, length.out = max(n_init * 10, 50))\n  fvals <- f(grid)\n  pos_idx <- which(fvals > 0)\n\n  if (length(pos_idx) < 2) {\n    stop(\"Could not find at least 2 points where f(x) > 0 in the search range.\")\n  }\n\n  sel <- pos_idx[seq(1, length(pos_idx), length.out = min(n_init, length(pos_idx)))]\n  x_init <- grid[sel]\n\n  mode_idx <- which.max(fvals)\n  mode_x <- grid[mode_idx]\n  if (!(mode_x %in% x_init) && fvals[mode_idx] > 0) {\n    x_init <- sort(unique(c(x_init, mode_x)))\n  }\n\n  return(x_init)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Main function: Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, x_init = NULL) {\n  # --- Input Validation --- #\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub, x_init)\n\n  # --- Choose initial abscissae if not provided --- #\n  if (is.null(x_init)) {\n    x_init <- choose_initial_abscissae(f, lb, ub)\n  }\n  x_init <- sort(unique(x_init))\n\n  # --- Initialize --- #\n  x_abs <- x_init\n  h_vals <- eval_log_density(f, x_abs)\n\n  # --- Check initial log-concavity --- #\n  if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n    stop(\"Density does not appear to be log-concave based on initial abscissae.\")\n  }\n\n  # --- Build initial upper hull --- #\n  upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n\n  # --- Sampling loop --- #\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  count <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (count < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Step 1: Sample from upper envelope\n    proposal <- sample_upper_hull(upper_hull)\n    x_star <- proposal$x\n    u_x_star <- proposal$u_x\n\n    # Safety: skip NaN proposals\n    if (!is.finite(x_star) || !is.finite(u_x_star)) next\n\n    # Step 2: Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    l_x_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, h_vals, x_abs)\n\n    if (is.finite(l_x_star) && log(w) <= l_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n      next\n    }\n\n    # Step 3: Rejection test — evaluate h(x*)\n    h_x_star <- eval_log_density(f, x_star)\n\n    if (log(w) <= h_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n    }\n\n    # Step 4: Update abscissae (only if h is finite — skip zero-density points)\n    if (is.finite(h_x_star)) {\n      ins_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n      h_vals <- append(h_vals, h_x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n\n    # Remove near-duplicates for numerical stability\n    dedup <- deduplicate_abscissae(x_abs, h_vals)\n    x_abs <- dedup$x\n    h_vals <- dedup$h\n\n    # Step 5: Check log-concavity\n    if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n      stop(\"Log-concavity violated after adding a new point. The density is not log-concave.\")\n    }\n\n    # Step 6: Rebuild upper hull\n    upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n  }\n\n  if (count < n) {\n    warning(paste(\"Only generated\", count, \"out of\", n, \"requested samples.\"))\n    samples <- samples[1:count]\n  }\n\n  return(samples)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Test function: formal testing with known distributions\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  report <- function(name, passed, info = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": PASS\"), \"\\n\")\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": FAIL\"), \"\\n\")\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(info) > 0) cat(\"  \", info, \"\\n\")\n  }\n\n  # ---- Test 1: Standard Normal N(0,1) ---- #\n  cat(\"--- Test 1: Standard Normal N(0,1) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf)\n    m <- mean(samples); s <- sd(samples)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~0), SD = %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", m, s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pnorm\")\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m) < 0.1 && abs(s - 1) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n    writeLines(as.character(samples), \"/app/normal_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved 10000 samples to /app/normal_samples.txt\\n\")\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  # check log-concavity at the current abscissae\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ncheck_log_concavity <- function(h_vals, x_vals) {\n  n <- length(x_vals)\n  if (n < 3) return(TRUE)\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  dh <- diff(h_vals) / diff(x_vals)\n  # Log-concavity requires non-increasing slopes\n  for (i in 2:length(dh)) {\n    if (is.finite(dh[i]) && is.finite(dh[i - 1])) {\n      if (dh[i] > dh[i - 1] + 1e-6) {\n        return(FALSE)\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  return(TRUE)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: remove near-duplicate abscissae to avoid numerical issues\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ndeduplicate_abscissae <- function(x_vals, h_vals, tol = 1e-10) {\n  keep <- rep(TRUE, length(x_vals))\n  for (i in 2:length(x_vals)) {\n    if (abs(x_vals[i] - x_vals[i - 1]) < tol) {\n      keep[i] <- FALSE\n    }\n  }\n  list(x = x_vals[keep], h = h_vals[keep])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: build the upper hull using secant-based tangent approximation\n#\n# Uses the formulation from Gilks & Wild (1992):\n# - For interior points j (2..k-1), the \"tangent\" slope at x_j is approximated\n#   by the slope of the line from (x_{j-1}, h_{j-1}) to (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1}).\n# - For endpoint j=1: slope of secant to x_2.\n# - For endpoint j=k: slope of secant from x_{k-1}.\n#\n# The intersection points z_j between consecutive tangent lines define the\n# piecewise domains.\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nbuild_upper_hull <- function(h_vals, x_vals, lb, ub) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (k < 2) stop(\"Need at least 2 abscissae to build the envelope.\")\n\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  sec <- diff(h_vals) / diff(x_vals)\n\n  # Approximate derivative at each abscissa\n  hprime <- numeric(k)\n  if (k == 2) {\n    hprime[1] <- sec[1]\n    hprime[2] <- sec[1]\n  } else {\n    hprime[1] <- sec[1]\n    hprime[k] <- sec[k - 1]\n    for (j in 2:(k - 1)) {\n      # Use slope through (x_{j-1}, h_{j-1}) and (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1})\n      hprime[j] <- (h_vals[j + 1] - h_vals[j - 1]) / (x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j - 1])\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Check boundary conditions for integrability\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && lb < 0) {\n    if (!is.finite(hprime[1]) || hprime[1] <= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have positive slope at the leftmost abscissa when lb = -Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n  if (is.infinite(ub) && ub > 0) {\n    if (!is.finite(hprime[k]) || hprime[k] >= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have negative slope at the rightmost abscissa when ub = Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Tangent lines: u_j(x) = h_j + hprime_j * (x - x_j) = intercept_j + slope_j * x\n  slopes <- hprime\n  intercepts <- h_vals - hprime * x_vals\n\n  # Intersection points z between consecutive tangent lines\n  z <- numeric(k + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[k + 1] <- ub\n  for (j in seq_len(k - 1)) {\n    denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n    if (abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n      z[j + 1] <- (x_vals[j] + x_vals[j + 1]) / 2\n    } else {\n      z[j + 1] <- (intercepts[j + 1] - intercepts[j]) / denom\n    }\n  }\n\n  return(list(slopes = slopes, intercepts = intercepts, z = z))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: evaluate the lower hull (chord through consecutive abscissae)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\neval_lower_hull <- function(x, h_vals, x_vals) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (x < x_vals[1] || x > x_vals[k]) return(-Inf)\n  j <- findInterval(x, x_vals, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  if (j == 0) j <- 1\n  if (j >= k) j <- k - 1\n  dx <- x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j]\n  if (abs(dx) < 1e-15) return(h_vals[j])\n  t <- (x - x_vals[j]) / dx\n  return((1 - t) * h_vals[j] + t * h_vals[j + 1])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: sample from the piecewise-exponential upper envelope\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nsample_upper_hull <- function(upper_hull) {\n  slopes <- upper_hull$slopes\n  intercepts <- upper_hull$intercepts\n  z <- upper_hull$z\n  k <- length(slopes)\n\n  # Compute log of the integral of exp(s*x + c) on each piece [a, b]\n  log_areas <- numeric(k)\n  for (j in 1:k) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    s <- slopes[j]\n    c_val <- intercepts[j]\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * b - log(s)\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a - log(-s)\n    } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + log(b - a)\n    } else {\n      # log(integral) = c + s*a + log(|expm1(s*(b-a))|) - log(|s|)\n      delta <- s * (b - a)\n      if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n        # Taylor approximation for small delta\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * (a + b) / 2 + log(b - a)\n      } else {\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a + log(abs(expm1(delta))) - log(abs(s))\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Filter out non-finite log_areas (shouldn't happen, but safety)\n  valid <- is.finite(log_areas)\n  if (!any(valid)) stop(\"All envelope pieces have non-finite area.\")\n\n  # Normalize to get probabilities\n  max_log <- max(log_areas[valid])\n  areas <- rep(0, k)\n  areas[valid] <- exp(log_areas[valid] - max_log)\n  probs <- areas / sum(areas)\n\n  # Sample which piece\n  j <- sample.int(k, size = 1, prob = probs)\n\n  a <- z[j]\n  b <- z[j + 1]\n  s <- slopes[j]\n  u <- runif(1)\n\n  if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n    x_star <- b + log(u) / s\n  } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n    x_star <- a + log(1 - u) / s\n  } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n    x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n  } else {\n    delta <- s * (b - a)\n    if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n      x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      x_star <- a + log(1 + u * expm1(delta)) / s\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Evaluate upper hull at x_star\n  u_x <- s * x_star + intercepts[j]\n  return(list(x = x_star, u_x = u_x))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: validate inputs\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub, x_init) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || n < 1 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be less than 'ub'.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.null(x_init)) {\n    if (!is.numeric(x_init) || length(x_init) < 2) {\n      stop(\"'x_init' must be a numeric vector with at least 2 elements.\")\n    }\n    if (any(x_init <= lb) || any(x_init >= ub)) {\n      stop(\"All initial abscissae must be strictly inside (lb, ub).\")\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: choose initial abscissae automatically\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nchoose_initial_abscissae <- function(f, lb, ub, n_init = 5) {\n  left <- if (is.infinite(lb)) -10 else lb + 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  right <- if (is.infinite(ub)) 10 else ub - 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) { left <- -10; right <- 10 }\n\n  grid <- seq(left, right, length.out = max(n_init * 10, 50))\n  fvals <- f(grid)\n  pos_idx <- which(fvals > 0)\n\n  if (length(pos_idx) < 2) {\n    stop(\"Could not find at least 2 points where f(x) > 0 in the search range.\")\n  }\n\n  sel <- pos_idx[seq(1, length(pos_idx), length.out = min(n_init, length(pos_idx)))]\n  x_init <- grid[sel]\n\n  mode_idx <- which.max(fvals)\n  mode_x <- grid[mode_idx]\n  if (!(mode_x %in% x_init) && fvals[mode_idx] > 0) {\n    x_init <- sort(unique(c(x_init, mode_x)))\n  }\n\n  return(x_init)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Main function: Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, x_init = NULL) {\n  # --- Input Validation --- #\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub, x_init)\n\n  # --- Choose initial abscissae if not provided --- #\n  if (is.null(x_init)) {\n    x_init <- choose_initial_abscissae(f, lb, ub)\n  }\n  x_init <- sort(unique(x_init))\n\n  # --- Initialize --- #\n  x_abs <- x_init\n  h_vals <- eval_log_density(f, x_abs)\n\n  # --- Check initial log-concavity --- #\n  if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n    stop(\"Density does not appear to be log-concave based on initial abscissae.\")\n  }\n\n  # --- Build initial upper hull --- #\n  upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n\n  # --- Sampling loop --- #\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  count <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (count < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Step 1: Sample from upper envelope\n    proposal <- sample_upper_hull(upper_hull)\n    x_star <- proposal$x\n    u_x_star <- proposal$u_x\n\n    # Safety: skip NaN proposals\n    if (!is.finite(x_star) || !is.finite(u_x_star)) next\n\n    # Step 2: Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    l_x_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, h_vals, x_abs)\n\n    if (is.finite(l_x_star) && log(w) <= l_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n      next\n    }\n\n    # Step 3: Rejection test — evaluate h(x*)\n    h_x_star <- eval_log_density(f, x_star)\n\n    if (log(w) <= h_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n    }\n\n    # Step 4: Update abscissae (only if h is finite — skip zero-density points)\n    if (is.finite(h_x_star)) {\n      ins_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n      h_vals <- append(h_vals, h_x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n\n      # Remove near-duplicates for numerical stability\n      dedup <- deduplicate_abscissae(x_abs, h_vals)\n      x_abs <- dedup$x\n      h_vals <- dedup$h\n\n      # Step 5: Check log-concavity\n      if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n        stop(\"Log-concavity violated after adding a new point. The density is not log-concave.\")\n      }\n\n      # Step 6: Rebuild upper hull\n      upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (count < n) {\n    warning(paste(\"Only generated\", count, \"out of\", n, \"requested samples.\"))\n    samples <- samples[1:count]\n  }\n\n  return(samples)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Test function: formal testing with known distributions\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  report <- function(name, passed, info = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": PASS\"), \"\\n\")\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": FAIL\"), \"\\n\")\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(info) > 0) cat(\"  \", info, \"\\n\")\n  }\n\n  # ---- Test 1: Standard Normal N(0,1) ---- #\n  cat(\"--- Test 1: Standard Normal N(0,1) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf)\n    m <- mean(samples); s <- sd(samples)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~0), SD = %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", m, s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pnorm\")\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m) < 0.1 && abs(s - 1) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n    writeLines(as.character(samples), \"/app/normal_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved 10000 samples to /app/normal_samples.txt\\n\")\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  # --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: remove near-duplicate abscissae to avoid numerical issues\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ndeduplicate_abscissae <- function(x_vals, h_vals, tol = 1e-10) {\n  keep <- rep(TRUE, length(x_vals))\n  for (i in 2:length(x_vals)) {\n    if (abs(x_vals[i] - x_vals[i - 1]) < tol) {\n      keep[i] <- FALSE\n    }\n  }\n  list(x = x_vals[keep], h = h_vals[keep])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: build the upper hull using secant-based tangent approximation\n#\n# Uses the formulation from Gilks & Wild (1992):\n# - For interior points j (2..k-1), the \"tangent\" slope at x_j is approximated\n#   by the slope of the line from (x_{j-1}, h_{j-1}) to (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1}).\n# - For endpoint j=1: slope of secant to x_2.\n# - For endpoint j=k: slope of secant from x_{k-1}.\n#\n# The intersection points z_j between consecutive tangent lines define the\n# piecewise domains.\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nbuild_upper_hull <- function(h_vals, x_vals, lb, ub) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (k < 2) stop(\"Need at least 2 abscissae to build the envelope.\")\n\n  # Secant slopes between consecutive points\n  sec <- diff(h_vals) / diff(x_vals)\n\n  # Approximate derivative at each abscissa\n  hprime <- numeric(k)\n  if (k == 2) {\n    hprime[1] <- sec[1]\n    hprime[2] <- sec[1]\n  } else {\n    hprime[1] <- sec[1]\n    hprime[k] <- sec[k - 1]\n    for (j in 2:(k - 1)) {\n      # Use slope through (x_{j-1}, h_{j-1}) and (x_{j+1}, h_{j+1})\n      hprime[j] <- (h_vals[j + 1] - h_vals[j - 1]) / (x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j - 1])\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Check boundary conditions for integrability\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && lb < 0) {\n    if (!is.finite(hprime[1]) || hprime[1] <= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have positive slope at the leftmost abscissa when lb = -Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n  if (is.infinite(ub) && ub > 0) {\n    if (!is.finite(hprime[k]) || hprime[k] >= 0) {\n      stop(\"Log-density must have negative slope at the rightmost abscissa when ub = Inf.\")\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Tangent lines: u_j(x) = h_j + hprime_j * (x - x_j) = intercept_j + slope_j * x\n  slopes <- hprime\n  intercepts <- h_vals - hprime * x_vals\n\n  # Intersection points z between consecutive tangent lines\n  z <- numeric(k + 1)\n  z[1] <- lb\n  z[k + 1] <- ub\n  for (j in seq_len(k - 1)) {\n    denom <- slopes[j] - slopes[j + 1]\n    if (!is.finite(denom) || abs(denom) < 1e-15) {\n      z[j + 1] <- (x_vals[j] + x_vals[j + 1]) / 2\n    } else {\n      z_candidate <- (intercepts[j + 1] - intercepts[j]) / denom\n      if (!is.finite(z_candidate)) {\n        z[j + 1] <- (x_vals[j] + x_vals[j + 1]) / 2\n      } else {\n        z[j + 1] <- z_candidate\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return(list(slopes = slopes, intercepts = intercepts, z = z))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: evaluate the lower hull (chord through consecutive abscissae)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\neval_lower_hull <- function(x, h_vals, x_vals) {\n  k <- length(x_vals)\n  if (x < x_vals[1] || x > x_vals[k]) return(-Inf)\n  j <- findInterval(x, x_vals, rightmost.closed = TRUE)\n  if (j == 0) j <- 1\n  if (j >= k) j <- k - 1\n  dx <- x_vals[j + 1] - x_vals[j]\n  if (abs(dx) < 1e-15) return(h_vals[j])\n  t <- (x - x_vals[j]) / dx\n  return((1 - t) * h_vals[j] + t * h_vals[j + 1])\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: sample from the piecewise-exponential upper envelope\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nsample_upper_hull <- function(upper_hull) {\n  slopes <- upper_hull$slopes\n  intercepts <- upper_hull$intercepts\n  z <- upper_hull$z\n  k <- length(slopes)\n\n  # Compute log of the integral of exp(s*x + c) on each piece [a, b]\n  log_areas <- numeric(k)\n  for (j in 1:k) {\n    a <- z[j]\n    b <- z[j + 1]\n    s <- slopes[j]\n    c_val <- intercepts[j]\n\n    if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * b - log(s)\n    } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a - log(-s)\n    } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n      log_areas[j] <- c_val + log(b - a)\n    } else {\n      # log(integral) = c + s*a + log(|expm1(s*(b-a))|) - log(|s|)\n      delta <- s * (b - a)\n      if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n        # Taylor approximation for small delta\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * (a + b) / 2 + log(b - a)\n      } else {\n        log_areas[j] <- c_val + s * a + log(abs(expm1(delta))) - log(abs(s))\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Filter out non-finite log_areas (shouldn't happen, but safety)\n  valid <- is.finite(log_areas)\n  if (!any(valid)) stop(\"All envelope pieces have non-finite area.\")\n\n  # Normalize to get probabilities\n  max_log <- max(log_areas[valid])\n  areas <- rep(0, k)\n  areas[valid] <- exp(log_areas[valid] - max_log)\n  probs <- areas / sum(areas)\n\n  # Sample which piece\n  j <- sample.int(k, size = 1, prob = probs)\n\n  a <- z[j]\n  b <- z[j + 1]\n  s <- slopes[j]\n  u <- runif(1)\n\n  if (is.infinite(a) && a < 0) {\n    x_star <- b + log(u) / s\n  } else if (is.infinite(b) && b > 0) {\n    x_star <- a + log(1 - u) / s\n  } else if (abs(s) < 1e-15) {\n    x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n  } else {\n    delta <- s * (b - a)\n    if (abs(delta) < 1e-10) {\n      x_star <- a + u * (b - a)\n    } else {\n      x_star <- a + log(1 + u * expm1(delta)) / s\n    }\n  }\n\n  # Evaluate upper hull at x_star\n  u_x <- s * x_star + intercepts[j]\n  return(list(x = x_star, u_x = u_x))\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: validate inputs\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nvalidate_inputs <- function(n, f, lb, ub, x_init) {\n  if (!is.numeric(n) || length(n) != 1 || n < 1 || n != floor(n)) {\n    stop(\"'n' must be a positive integer.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.function(f)) {\n    stop(\"'f' must be a function.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(lb) || length(lb) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.numeric(ub) || length(ub) != 1) {\n    stop(\"'ub' must be a single numeric value.\")\n  }\n  if (lb >= ub) {\n    stop(\"'lb' must be less than 'ub'.\")\n  }\n  if (!is.null(x_init)) {\n    if (!is.numeric(x_init) || length(x_init) < 2) {\n      stop(\"'x_init' must be a numeric vector with at least 2 elements.\")\n    }\n    if (any(x_init <= lb) || any(x_init >= ub)) {\n      stop(\"All initial abscissae must be strictly inside (lb, ub).\")\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Helper: choose initial abscissae automatically\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nchoose_initial_abscissae <- function(f, lb, ub, n_init = 5) {\n  left <- if (is.infinite(lb)) -10 else lb + 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  right <- if (is.infinite(ub)) 10 else ub - 0.01 * abs(ub - lb)\n  if (is.infinite(lb) && is.infinite(ub)) { left <- -10; right <- 10 }\n\n  grid <- seq(left, right, length.out = max(n_init * 10, 50))\n  fvals <- f(grid)\n  pos_idx <- which(fvals > 0)\n\n  if (length(pos_idx) < 2) {\n    stop(\"Could not find at least 2 points where f(x) > 0 in the search range.\")\n  }\n\n  sel <- pos_idx[seq(1, length(pos_idx), length.out = min(n_init, length(pos_idx)))]\n  x_init <- grid[sel]\n\n  mode_idx <- which.max(fvals)\n  mode_x <- grid[mode_idx]\n  if (!(mode_x %in% x_init) && fvals[mode_idx] > 0) {\n    x_init <- sort(unique(c(x_init, mode_x)))\n  }\n\n  return(x_init)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Main function: Adaptive Rejection Sampling\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\nars <- function(n, f, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf, x_init = NULL) {\n  # --- Input Validation --- #\n  validate_inputs(n, f, lb, ub, x_init)\n\n  # --- Choose initial abscissae if not provided --- #\n  if (is.null(x_init)) {\n    x_init <- choose_initial_abscissae(f, lb, ub)\n  }\n  x_init <- sort(unique(x_init))\n\n  # --- Initialize --- #\n  x_abs <- x_init\n  h_vals <- eval_log_density(f, x_abs)\n\n  # --- Check initial log-concavity --- #\n  if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n    stop(\"Density does not appear to be log-concave based on initial abscissae.\")\n  }\n\n  # --- Build initial upper hull --- #\n  upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n\n  # --- Sampling loop --- #\n  samples <- numeric(n)\n  count <- 0\n  max_iter <- n * 100\n  iter <- 0\n\n  while (count < n && iter < max_iter) {\n    iter <- iter + 1\n\n    # Step 1: Sample from upper envelope\n    proposal <- sample_upper_hull(upper_hull)\n    x_star <- proposal$x\n    u_x_star <- proposal$u_x\n\n    # Safety: skip NaN proposals\n    if (!is.finite(x_star) || !is.finite(u_x_star)) next\n\n    # Step 2: Squeeze test\n    w <- runif(1)\n    l_x_star <- eval_lower_hull(x_star, h_vals, x_abs)\n\n    if (is.finite(l_x_star) && log(w) <= l_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n      next\n    }\n\n    # Step 3: Rejection test — evaluate h(x*)\n    h_x_star <- eval_log_density(f, x_star)\n\n    if (log(w) <= h_x_star - u_x_star) {\n      count <- count + 1\n      samples[count] <- x_star\n    }\n\n    # Step 4: Update abscissae (only if h is finite — skip zero-density points)\n    if (is.finite(h_x_star)) {\n      ins_pos <- findInterval(x_star, x_abs) + 1\n      x_abs <- append(x_abs, x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n      h_vals <- append(h_vals, h_x_star, after = ins_pos - 1)\n\n      # Remove near-duplicates for numerical stability\n      dedup <- deduplicate_abscissae(x_abs, h_vals)\n      x_abs <- dedup$x\n      h_vals <- dedup$h\n\n      # Step 5: Check log-concavity\n      if (!check_log_concavity(h_vals, x_abs)) {\n        stop(\"Log-concavity violated after adding a new point. The density is not log-concave.\")\n      }\n\n      # Step 6: Rebuild upper hull\n      upper_hull <- build_upper_hull(h_vals, x_abs, lb, ub)\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (count < n) {\n    warning(paste(\"Only generated\", count, \"out of\", n, \"requested samples.\"))\n    samples <- samples[1:count]\n  }\n\n  return(samples)\n}\n\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\n# Test function: formal testing with known distributions\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------- #\ntest <- function() {\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\")\n  cat(\"  Adaptive Rejection Sampler - Test Suite\\n\")\n  cat(\"============================================\\n\\n\")\n\n  pass_count <- 0\n  fail_count <- 0\n\n  report <- function(name, passed, info = \"\") {\n    if (passed) {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": PASS\"), \"\\n\")\n      pass_count <<- pass_count + 1\n    } else {\n      cat(paste0(name, \": FAIL\"), \"\\n\")\n      fail_count <<- fail_count + 1\n    }\n    if (nchar(info) > 0) cat(\"  \", info, \"\\n\")\n  }\n\n  # ---- Test 1: Standard Normal N(0,1) ---- #\n  cat(\"--- Test 1: Standard Normal N(0,1) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = dnorm, lb = -Inf, ub = Inf)\n    m <- mean(samples); s <- sd(samples)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~0), SD = %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", m, s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pnorm\")\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m) < 0.1 && abs(s - 1) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n    writeLines(as.character(samples), \"/app/normal_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved 10000 samples to /app/normal_samples.txt\\n\")\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_normal_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  # ---- Test 2: Exponential(rate=1) ---- #\n  cat(\"--- Test 2: Exponential(rate=1) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = dexp, lb = 0, ub = Inf,\n                   x_init = c(0.1, 1, 3, 5))\n    m <- mean(samples); s <- sd(samples)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~1), SD = %.4f (expected ~1)\\n\", m, s))\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pexp\")\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m - 1) < 0.15 && abs(s - 1) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_exponential_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n    writeLines(as.character(samples), \"/app/exponential_samples.txt\")\n    cat(\"  Saved 10000 samples to /app/exponential_samples.txt\\n\")\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_exponential_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  # ---- Test 3: Gamma(shape=3, rate=2) ---- #\n  cat(\"--- Test 3: Gamma(shape=3, rate=2) ---\\n\")\n  set.seed(42)\n  tryCatch({\n    f_gamma <- function(x) dgamma(x, shape = 3, rate = 2)\n    samples <- ars(n = 10000, f = f_gamma, lb = 0, ub = Inf,\n                   x_init = c(0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 4))\n    m <- mean(samples); s <- sd(samples)\n    true_mean <- 3 / 2; true_sd <- sqrt(3) / 2\n    cat(sprintf(\"  Sample mean = %.4f (expected ~%.4f), SD = %.4f (expected ~%.4f)\\n\",\n                m, true_mean, s, true_sd))\n    ks <- ks.test(samples, \"pgamma\", shape = 3, rate = 2)\n    cat(sprintf(\"  KS test p-value = %.4f\\n\", ks$p.value))\n    passed <- abs(m - true_mean) < 0.15 && abs(s - true_sd) < 0.15 && ks$p.value > 0.01\n    report(\"test_gamma_distribution\", passed,\n           sprintf(\"mean=%.4f, sd=%.4f, ks_p=%.4f\", m, s, ks$p.value))\n  }, error = function(e) {\n    report(\"test_gamma_distribution\", FALSE, paste(\"Error:\", e$message))\n  })\n  cat(\"\\n\")\n\n  #
